***hilltop.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hilltop.html>hilltop</a> (92504)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hill</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">top</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hilltop.html>hilltop</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">hilltops</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The peak or crest of a hill.
<ul><li><b>1946</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bertrand_Russell" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Bertrand Russell">Bertrand Russell</a>, <i>History of Western Philosophy</i>, I.21:
<dl><dd>The territory should be small enough to be surveyed in its entirety from a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hilltop.html>hilltop</a></b>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>used attributively in phrases such as "a <a href = vnd.unilang:hilltop.html>hilltop</a> house"</li></ul>
</body>

***hinderen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hinderen.html>hinderen</a> (17843)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:hinderen.html>hinderen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*hindaron</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hinderōną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hinderen.html>hinderen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> hinder, impede</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be in the way, to be a problem</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:overgankelijk.html>overgankelijk</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voortgang.html>voortgang</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verstoren.html>verstoren</a></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hinken.html>hinken</a> (54291)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:hinken.html>hinken</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*hinkan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hinkaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hinken.html>hinken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to limp, to hobble (walk with difficulty due to injury)</li></ol>

***hippen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hippen.html>hippen</a> (105450)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:huppen.html>huppen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to hop</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hop</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">hüpfen</i>.

***hippocampus.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hippocampus.html>hippocampus</a> (51704)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:hippocampus.html>hippocampus</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἱππόκαμπος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">hippókampos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from
<i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ῐ̔́ππος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">híppos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">horse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κάμπος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kámpos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sea-monster</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The anatomy sense <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> so named from its resemblance to the seahorse.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hippocampus.html>hippocampus</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">hippocampi</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mythology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A mythological creature with the front head and forelimbs of a horse and the rear of a dolphin.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">hippocamp</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A part of the brain located inside the temporal lobe, consisting mainly of grey matter. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a component of the limbic system and plays a role in memory and emotion.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">neuroanatomy</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> HIPP</li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hippocampus.html>hippocampus</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:anatomie.html>anatomie</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:deel.html>deel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hersenen.html>hersenen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:betrokken.html>betrokken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geheugen.html>geheugen</a>, stress <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> ruimtelijke orriëntatie
<dl><dd><ul><li><i> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hippocampus.html>hippocampus</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:maakt.html>maakt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deel.html>deel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> limbische <a href = vnd.unilang:systeem.html>systeem</a></i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:historisch.html>historisch</a> (8430)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:historisch.html>historisch</a></i>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:historicus.html>historicus</a></i>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἱστορικός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">historikós</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The form borrowed from German replaced earlier forms ending on the equivalent of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-lijk</i>.
</p>

<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hit</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to murder</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-man</i>

***hitte.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hitte.html>hitte</a> (3855)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:hitte.html>hitte</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*hitta</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hitjō</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Hitze</i>. Now commonly interpreted as <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heet.html>heet</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-te</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ness</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Also related with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">heat</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hitte.html>hitte</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>

title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">कूप</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kū́pa</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cave</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kew-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bend, curve</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The computing term <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> chosen as an in-joke relating to bees; see <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://blogs.msdn.com/b/oldnewthing/archive/2003/08/08/54618.aspx">[1]</a>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hive.html>hive</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hives.html>hives</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A structure, whether artificial or natural, for housing a swarm of honeybees.
<ul><li><b>1709</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Dryden" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:John Dryden">John Dryden</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/The_Works_of_Virgil_(Dryden)/Georgics_(Dryden)" class="extiw" title="s:The Works of Virgil (Dryden)/Georgics (Dryden)">Georgics</a></i> IV.10-13:
<dl><dd><i>First, for thy Bees a quiet Station find,</i></dd>
<dd>And lodge 'em under Covert of the Wind:</dd>
<dd>For <a href = vnd.unilang:winds.html>Winds</a>, when homeward they return, will drive</dd>
<dd>The loaded <a href = vnd.unilang:carriers.html>Carriers</a> from their Ev'<a href = vnd.unilang:ning.html>ning</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hive.html>Hive</a></b>.<i></i></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>The bees of one <a href = vnd.unilang:hive.html>hive</a>; a swarm of bees.
<ul><li><b>c. 1602</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Troilus_and_Cressida" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Troilus and Cressida">Troilus and Cressida</a></i>, Act I, Scene iii:
<dl><dd>When that the general <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not like the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hive.html>hive</a></b>, to whom the foragers shall all repair, what honey <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> expected?</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A place swarming with busy occupants; a crowd.
<ul><li><b>?</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alfred_Tennyson" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Alfred Tennyson">Alfred Tennyson</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Boadicea" class="extiw" title="s:Boadicea">Boadicea</a></i>
<dl><dd>There the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hive.html>hive</a></b> of Roman liars worship a gluttonous emperor-idiot.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing<span class="ib-comma">,</span> Microsoft <a href = vnd.unilang:windows.html>Windows</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A section of the registry.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2006</b>,  Jean Andrews,  <cite>Fixing <a href = vnd.unilang:windows.html>Windows</a> XP</cite>, page 352:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:windows.html>Windows</a> builds the registry from the five registry <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hives.html>hives</a></b><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>2011</b>, Samuel Phung, <i>Professional Microsoft <a href = vnd.unilang:windows.html>Windows</a> Embedded CE 6.0</i>
<dl><dd>For devices built with hive-based registry implementation, the registry data are broken into three different <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hives.html>hives</a></b> — the <a href = vnd.unilang:boot.html>boot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hive.html>hive</a>, system <a href = vnd.unilang:hive.html>hive</a>, and user <a href = vnd.unilang:hive.html>hive</a>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hive.html>hive</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hives.html>hives</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">hiving</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">hived</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> entomology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To enter or possess a <a href = vnd.unilang:hive.html>hive</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To form a hive-like entity.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To collect into a <a href = vnd.unilang:hive.html>hive</a>.
<dl><dd><i>to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hive.html>hive</a></b> a swarm of bees</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To store in a <a href = vnd.unilang:hive.html>hive</a> or similarly.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>181</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lord_Byron" class="extiw" title="w:Lord Byron">Lord Byron</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Childe_Harold%27s_Pilgrimage" class="extiw" title="w:Childe Harold | s Pilgrimage"><a href = vnd.unilang:chillen.html>Childe</a> Harold’s Pilgrimage. </a></cite>, London |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Murray_(publisher)" class="extiw" title="w:John Murray (publisher)">John Murray</a>,, canto 3<span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(please specify the stanza number)</span>:</span><dl><dd></dd></dl></div>
<dl><dd><b>Hiving</b> wisdom with each studious year.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To take shelter or lodgings together; to reside in a collective body.
<ul><li><b>1596-97</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Merchant_of_Venice" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Merchant of Venice">The Merchant of Venice</a></i>, Act II, Scene v<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.opensourceshakespeare.org/views/plays/play_view.php?WorkID=merchantveniceamp;Scope=entireamp;pleasewait=1amp;msg=pl">[2]</a></sup>:
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:shylock.html>Shylock</a>:</dd>
<dd>The patch <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> enough, but a huge feeder,</dd>
<dd>Snail-slow in profit, and he <a href = vnd.unilang:sleeps.html>sleeps</a> by day</dd>
<dd>More than the wild-cat; <a href = vnd.unilang:drones.html>drones</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hive.html>hive</a></b> not with <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>;</dd>
<dd>Therefore I part with him; and part with him</dd>
<dd>To one what I would have him help to waste</dd>
<dd>His borrowed purse. <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1725</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alexander_Pope" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Alexander Pope">Alexander Pope</a>, letter to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Martha_Blount" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Martha Blount">Martha Blount</a>
<dl><dd><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>to get into <a href = vnd.unilang:warmer.html>warmer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:houses.html>houses</a>, and <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hive.html>hive</a></b> together in cities</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hobbelig.html>hobbelig</a> (25333)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hobbel.html>hobbel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bump</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i>.
</p>

***hocus-pocus.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hocus-pocus.html>hocus-pocus</a> (30511)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Dates from the 17th century when used by jugglers and magicians as a nonsense magical incantation.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup> Some believe it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a corruption of <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> from the Roman Catholic liturgy of the Eucharist, <i><b>hoc est</b> enim <b>corpus</b> meum</i>, although this <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> disputed. Accroding to Microsoft® Encarta® 2009, it <a href = vnd.unilang:comes.html>comes</a> from Pseudo-Latin <i>hax pax <a href = vnd.unilang:max.html>max</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deus.html>Deus</a> adimax</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hocus-pocus.html>hocus-pocus</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>A phrase used as a magical incantation to bring about some change.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hocus-pocus.html>hocus-pocus</a></strong> (<i>usually uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">hocus-pocuses</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Trickery or nonsense.
<dl><dd><i>What <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hocus-pocus.html>hocus-pocus</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> this?</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete<span class="ib-comma">,</span> countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A conjurer.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete<span class="ib-comma">,</span> countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A conjurer's trick.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hocus-pocus.html>hocus-pocus</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">hocus-pocuses</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">hocus-pocusing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">hocus-pocused</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To cheat.
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of L'Estrange to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hocus-pocus.html>hocus-pocus</a></b>

<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:verouderde.html>verouderde</a> spelling of <a href = vnd.unilang:vorm.html>vorm</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hocus.html>hocus</a> pocus <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> vóór 2006</li></ol>

***hoede.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoede.html>hoede</a> (5086)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoede.html>hoede</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoede.html>hoede</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoede.html>hoedes</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>heed, guard, alertness
<ul><li><b>1877</b>, H.A.M. Roelants, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:geschiedenis.html>Geschiedenis</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:consulaat.html>Consulaat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:keizerrijk.html>Keizerrijk</a></i>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoe.html>Hoe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verder.html>verder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:trekt.html>trekt</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:hoe.html>hoe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> krachtderarmees <a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verminderd.html>verminderd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> vermoeienis, <a href = vnd.unilang:verspreiding.html>verspreiding</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:noodzakelijkheid.html>noodzakelijkheid</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoede.html>hoede</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The further one marches, the more the armies' power decreases through fatigue, dispersion and the necessity to be on <b>guard</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>protection, care, auspices
<ul><li><b>1875</b>, translation of <i>The Lamplighter</i> by <a href = vnd.unilang:maria.html>Maria</a> Susanna Cummins.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl">Amalia <a href = vnd.unilang:gevoelen.html>gevoelde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gegrond.html>gegronde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bezwaar.html>bezwaar</a>; want <a href = vnd.unilang:hoewel.html>hoewel</a> jufvrouw Ellis <a href = vnd.unilang:gedurende.html>gedurende</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hunne.html>hunne</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:afwezigheid.html>afwezigheid</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zou.html>zou</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:blijven.html>blijven</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:wist.html>wist</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>zij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrouw.html>vrouw</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:zelfs.html>zelfs</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a> mogt <a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>zij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gewillig.html>gewillig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> Geertrui <a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoede.html>hoede</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nemen.html>nemen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zeer.html>zeer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ongeschikt.html>ongeschikt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:persoon.html>persoon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zou.html>zou</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meisje.html>meisje</a> in den <a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>harer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eerste.html>eerste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:droefheid.html>droefheid</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:troosten.html>troosten</a>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Amalia understood this objection <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> justified; <li>remit, scope of control
<dl><dd>René Stender <a href = vnd.unilang:legt.html>legt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:welke.html>welke</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zwembaden.html>zwembaden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:allemaal.html>allemaal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoede.html>hoede</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:commissie.html>commissie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vallen.html>vallen</a>.<br /><i>René Stender explains which swimming <a href = vnd.unilang:pools.html>pools</a> are within the <b>remit</b> of the commission.</i> – <a href = vnd.unilang:nen.html>Nen</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.nen.nl/NEN-Shop/Nieuwsberichten-Consumentenzaken/Interview-Zwembadnormen-verhogen-veiligheid.htm">Zwembadnormen <a href = vnd.unilang:verhogen.html>verhogen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:veiligheid.html>veiligheid</a></a> (2013)</dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoef.html>hoef</a> (767)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoef.html>hoef</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*huof</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hōfaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱoph₂ós</i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoef.html>hoef</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Huf</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hoof</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">hov</i>.

***hoefijzer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoefijzer.html>hoefijzer</a> (29279)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hoefisen</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoef.html>hoef</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hoof</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ijzer.html>ijzer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">iron</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoefijzer.html>hoefijzer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoefijzers.html>hoefijzers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoefijzer.html>hoefijzertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>horseshoe (metallic 'shoe' for an equine's hoof)</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***hoepelen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoepelen.html>hoepelen</a> (39441)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoepel.html>hoepel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoop.html>hoop</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoepelen.html>hoepelen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to roll <a href = vnd.unilang:hoops.html>hoops</a> <span class="defdate">[from 17th c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>1683</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:steven.html>Steven</a> Blankaart, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> Kartesiaanse <a href = vnd.unilang:academie.html>academie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ofte.html>ofte</a>, institutie <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> medicyne</i>, publ. by <a href = vnd.unilang:johannes.html>Johannes</a> ten <a href = vnd.unilang:hoorn.html>Hoorn</a>, page 205.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kinderen.html>kinderen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> datse <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> papsakken souden <a href = vnd.unilang:werden.html>werden</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebieden.html>gebieden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:spelen.html>spelen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wandelen.html>wandelen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:koten.html>koten</a>, knikkeren, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoepelen.html>hoepelen</a></b> amp;c. <a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> tyd <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jaar.html>jaar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mede.html>mede</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brengt.html>brengt</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werden.html>werden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sy.html>sy</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sterk.html>sterk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> vrolyk.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">One should command the children, so that they do not become fat-asses, to play, to walk, play with dice, play with <a href = vnd.unilang:marbles.html>marbles</a>, <b>roll <a href = vnd.unilang:hoops.html>hoops</a></b> amp;c. in accordance with the time of year, this <a href = vnd.unilang:makes.html>makes</a> them strong and happy.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to <a href = vnd.unilang:hula.html>hula</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoop.html>hoop</a> <span class="defdate">[from 20th c.]</span>

***hoerenzoon.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoerenzoon.html>hoerenzoon</a> (17496)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hoerensone</i>, first attested as a gloss for <i>manzer</i>, i.e. <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">mamzer</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoer.html>hoer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">whore, hooker</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">interfix</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zoon.html>zoon</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">son</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">whoreson</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Hurensohn</i> and the <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">huorresoan</i>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> perhaps calqued from the Dutch.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoerenzoon.html>hoerenzoon</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoerenzonen.html>hoerenzonen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoerenzoon.html>hoerenzoontje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> vulgar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">whoreson</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">son of a <a href = vnd.unilang:bitch.html>bitch</a></span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">despicable <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> son of a whore, <span class="Latn" lang="en">whoreson</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">son of a usually female prostitute</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoerenzoon.html>hoerenzoon</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoesten.html>hoesten</a> (11806)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoesten.html>hoesten</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*huoston</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hwōstōną</i>, derived from the strong verb <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hwōsaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kʷeh₂s-</i>.

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoesten.html>hoesten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To cough, push air from the lungs forcefully, as because of a cold</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To suffer from a (disease which causes a) cough</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To clear one's throat, notably by emulating the above</li></ol>
